Simple White Cake   1 cup white sugar Â½ cup butter 2 eggs 2 teaspoons vanilla extract 1â€‰Â½ cups all-purpose flour 1â€‰Â¾ teaspoons baking powder Â½ cup milk    Step 1  Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C). Grease and flour a 9x9 inch pan or line a muffin pan with paper liners. Step 2  In a medium bowl, cream together the sugar and butter. Beat in the eggs, one at a time, then stir in the vanilla.
